class="tocnumber">9</span><span class="toctext">External Links</span></a></li><li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-17"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">10</span><span class="toctext">References</span></a></li></ul></div></div><p><br></br></p><p>The <b>2018 WCS Montreal</b> is the fourth and last of four events of the <a href="/starcraft2/2018_StarCraft_II_World_Championship_Series#WCS_Circuit"title="2018 StarCraft II World Championship Series">2018 WCS Circuit</a>.<br></br>It takes place at DreamHack Montreal 2018 and is organized by <a href="/starcraft2/DreamHack"title="DreamHack">DreamHack</a>.
</p><h2><span class="mw-headline"id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/starcraft2/index.php?title=2018_WCS_Montreal&action=edit&section=1"title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2><p><b>First Group Stage</b>:
</p><ul><li>64 players in 16 groups of 4 players each, played in a dual tournament format</li><li>Matches are <abbr title="Best of 3">Bo3</abbr>.</li><li>Top 2 players of each group advance to the next stage.</li></ul><p><b>Second Group Stage</b>:
</p><ul><li>32 players in 8 groups of 4 players each, played in a dual tournament format</li><li>Matches are <abbr title="Best of 3">Bo3</abbr>.</li><li>Top 2 players of each group advance to the next stage.</li></ul><p><b>Third Group Stage</b>:
</p><ul><li>16 players from the Second Group Stage;</li><li>16 players from <a href="/starcraft2/2018_WCS_Montreal/Qualifiers"title="2018 WCS Montreal/Qualifiers">Qualifiers</a>.</li><li>8 groups of 4 players each, played in a dual tournament format.</li><li>Matches are <abbr title="Best of 3">Bo3</abbr>.</li><li>Top 2 players of each group advance to the playoffs.</li></ul><p><b>Playoffs</b>:
</p><ul><li>16 players in a single-elimination bracket</li><li>Round of 16 to Semifinals are played in <abbr title="Best of 5">Bo5</abbr>.</li><li>Finals are played in <abbr title="Best of 7">Bo7</abbr>.</li></ul><h3><span class="mw-headline"id="Map_Pool">Map Pool</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/starcraft2/index.php?title=2018_WCS_Montreal&action=edit&section=2"title="Edit section: Map Pool">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3><div
